  78:             "exp": exp_iso,
  79:             "pairing_id": _canon_uuid(pairing_id),
  80:             "protocol_version": 1,
  81:             "sender_broker_url": sender_broker_url,
  82:             "sender_id": _canon_uuid(sender_id),
  83:         },
  84:         sort_keys=True,
  85:         ensure_ascii=True,
  86:         separators=(",", ":"),
  87:     ).encode("utf-8")

  90: def bootstrap_key_id(bootstrap_pub_raw: bytes) -> bytes:
  91:     """SHA-256(bootstrap_pub)[:16] ג€” the broker uses this as a stable
  92:     identifier for the key version it should decrypt with. Lets the
  93:     sender rotate the key without affecting in-flight envelopes."""
  94:     if len(bootstrap_pub_raw) != 32:
  95:         raise ValueError("bootstrap_pub_raw must be 32 bytes")
  96:     return hashlib.sha256(bootstrap_pub_raw).digest()[:16]
  97: 
  98: 
  99: def decrypt_bootstrap_envelope(
 100:     *,
 101:     sender_bootstrap_priv: X25519PrivateKey,
 102:     sender_bootstrap_pub: bytes,
 103:     pairing_id: str,
 104:     sender_id: str,
 105:     sender_broker_url_from_trusted_state: str,
 106:     ephemeral_pubkey: bytes,
 107:     nonce: bytes,
 108:     ciphertext: bytes,
 109:     exp_iso: str,
 110:     bootstrap_key_id_b64_from_envelope: str,
 111:     now: datetime | None = None,
 112: ) -> tuple[str, bytes]:
 113:     """Decrypt one bootstrap envelope and return ``(user_id, pairing_key)``.
 114: 
 115:     ``sender_broker_url_from_trusted_state`` MUST come from the broker's
 116:     own pairing state ג€” NOT echoed from the envelope. Spec ֲ§9.3
 117:     security rule.
 118: 
 119:     Raises [BootstrapDecryptError] when:
 120:     - the bootstrap key id doesn't match (key was rotated between
 121:       device-build and broker-decrypt);
 122:     - the envelope's `exp` is outside ֲ±5min of `now`;
 123:     - AAD JSON canonical bytes diverge (i.e. ciphertext was bound to
 124:       different metadata, OR the syncler server tampered with
 125:       sender_broker_url);
 126:     - AES-GCM tag verification fails.
 127:     """
 128:     # Bootstrap key id rotation guard.
 129:     expected_kid = bootstrap_key_id(sender_bootstrap_pub)
 130:     expected_kid_b64 = _b64_std(expected_kid)
 131:     if bootstrap_key_id_b64_from_envelope != expected_kid_b64:
 132:         raise BootstrapDecryptError(
 133:             "bootstrap_key_id mismatch ג€” key was rotated since the device built this envelope",
 134:         )
 135: 
 136:     # Clock-skew window check (real replay guard is CAS at the broker).
 137:     now = now or datetime.now(UTC)
 138:     try:
 139:         exp = datetime.fromisoformat(exp_iso.replace("Z", "+00:00"))
 140:     except Exception as exc:
 141:         raise BootstrapDecryptError(f"invalid exp_iso: {exp_iso!r}") from exc
 142:     delta = (exp - now).total_seconds()
 143:     if abs(delta) > BROKER_CLOCK_SKEW_SECONDS:
 144:         raise BootstrapDecryptError(
 145:             f"exp outside ֲ±{BROKER_CLOCK_SKEW_SECONDS}s tolerance: delta={delta:.1f}s",
 146:         )
 147: 
 148:     # X25519 ECDH.
 149:     eph_pub = X25519PublicKey.from_public_bytes(ephemeral_pubkey)
 150:     shared_secret = sender_bootstrap_priv.exchange(eph_pub)
 151: 
 152:     # HKDF derivation. salt = eph_pub || sender_bootstrap_pub.
 153:     salt = ephemeral_pubkey + sender_bootstrap_pub
 154:     aead_key = HKDF(
 155:         algorithm=hashes.SHA256(),
 156:         length=32,
 157:         salt=salt,
 158:         info=_HKDF_INFO_BOOTSTRAP_AEAD,
 159:     ).derive(shared_secret)
 160: 
 161:     # Canonical AAD. sender_broker_url comes from TRUSTED STATE, not
 162:     # the envelope. This is the syncler-server-substitution guard.
 163:     aad = assemble_bootstrap_aad(
 164:         bootstrap_key_id_b64=expected_kid_b64,
 165:         exp_iso=exp_iso,
 166:         pairing_id=pairing_id,
 167:         sender_broker_url=sender_broker_url_from_trusted_state,
 168:         sender_id=sender_id,
 169:     )
 170: 
 171:     try:
 172:         plaintext = AESGCM(aead_key).decrypt(nonce, ciphertext, aad)
 173:     except InvalidTag as exc:
 174:         raise BootstrapDecryptError(
 175:             "AES-GCM tag verification failed ג€” AAD mismatch or tampered ciphertext",
 176:         ) from exc
 177: 
 178:     # Parse plaintext: {"user_id": "...", "pairing_key": "<base64 32>"}
 179:     try:
 180:         decoded = json.loads(plaintext.decode("utf-8"))
 181:         user_id = _canon_uuid(decoded["user_id"])
 182:         import base64 as _b64mod
 183:         pairing_key = _b64mod.b64decode(decoded["pairing_key"], validate=True)
 184:     except Exception as exc:
 185:         raise BootstrapDecryptError(
 186:             "bootstrap plaintext is not the expected {user_id, pairing_key} shape",
 187:         ) from exc
 188:     if len(pairing_key) != 32:
 189:         raise BootstrapDecryptError("decoded pairing_key is not 32 bytes")
 190:     return user_id, pairing_key
 191: 
 192: 
 193: def _b64_std(value: bytes) -> str:
 194:     import base64 as _b64mod
 195:     return _b64mod.b64encode(value).decode("ascii")
 196:

 201:     once at adoption, persist the private key (e.g. in their
 202:     secrets manager), and register the public key + signature via

 205:     priv = X25519PrivateKey.generate()

 succeeded in 349ms:
   1: """V1.5 automated pairing ג€” broker storage interface.
   2: 
   3: The sender-operated broker persists `(user_id, pairing_key)` keyed on
   4: `pairing_id` after successfully decrypting one bootstrap envelope.
   5: ``Client.wait_for_pairing(...)`` polls this storage to learn when a
   6: pairing has completed.
   7: 
   8: The protocol is sender-private. Production callers can plug in Redis,
   9: Postgres, or any other backing store; the SDK ships only the protocol
  10: + a default in-memory implementation for dev.
  11: """
  12: 
  13: from __future__ import annotations
  14: 
  15: import threading
  16: from dataclasses import dataclass
  17: from typing import Protocol
  18: 
  19: 
  20: @dataclass(frozen=True)
  21: class BrokerEntry:
  22:     """Completed pairing tuple stored by the broker after a successful
  23:     decrypt. The fields are exactly what `Client.set_pairing(...)`
  24:     needs to bring the SDK out of the pending state."""
  25:     user_id: str
  26:     pairing_key: bytes  # 32 bytes
  27: 
  28: 
  29: class BrokerStorageConflictError(Exception):
  30:     """Raised on compare-and-set conflict: same `pairing_id` already
  31:     completed with DIFFERENT `(user_id, pairing_key)` values. Indicates
  32:     a replay attack or a buggy device. Same values is idempotent ג€”
  33:     NOT a conflict (no exception)."""
  34: 
  35: 
  36: class BrokerStorage(Protocol):
  37:     """The broker storage protocol.
  38: 
  39:     Implementations MUST be thread-safe AND compare-and-set safe:
  40:     `complete(...)` is the syncronization point. The first call wins;
  41:     subsequent calls with identical values are idempotent; calls with
  42:     different values raise [BrokerStorageConflictError]. This semantics
  43:     is what defeats envelope replay (spec ֲ§9.3).
  44:     """
  45: 
  46:     def reserve(self, pairing_id: str) -> None:
  47:         """Called at `pairing/initiate` time to mark the slot. Optional
  48:         for in-memory storage; required for storages where you need
  49:         explicit slot creation (e.g. DB rows with not-null
  50:         constraints). Idempotent."""
  51: 
  52:     def complete(self, pairing_id: str, entry: BrokerEntry) -> None:
  53:         """Compare-and-set. Behavior:
  54: 
  55:         - First call for `pairing_id` ג†’ stores entry, returns.
  56:         - Second call with same `entry` ג†’ idempotent, returns.
  57:         - Second call with different `entry` ג†’
  58:           [BrokerStorageConflictError].
  59: 
  60:         Implementations MUST be atomic at the storage layer (Postgres
  61:         UPSERT WHERE NOT EXISTS or equivalent ג€” NOT a Python-level
  62:         check-then-store)."""
  63: 
  64:     def fetch(self, pairing_id: str) -> BrokerEntry | None:
  65:         """Returns the completed entry or `None` if still pending.
  66:         Called repeatedly by `Client.wait_for_pairing(...)`."""
  67: 
  68: 
  69: class InMemoryBrokerStorage:
  70:     """Default in-process implementation. Suitable for dev / tests /
  71:     single-process toy deployments. Loses state on restart. Not safe
  72:     across multiple uvicorn workers ג€” use a real storage backend
  73:     (Redis, Postgres) for production multi-worker setups.
  74:     """
  75: 
  76:     def __init__(self) -> None:
  77:         self._lock = threading.Lock()
  78:         self._entries: dict[str, BrokerEntry] = {}
  79: 
  80:     def reserve(self, pairing_id: str) -> None:
  81:         # No-op: dict permits any key. `complete` is the CAS point.
  82:         return None
  83: 
  84:     def complete(self, pairing_id: str, entry: BrokerEntry) -> None:
  85:         with self._lock:
  86:             existing = self._entries.get(pairing_id)
  87:             if existing is None:
  88:                 self._entries[pairing_id] = entry
  89:                 return
  90:             # Idempotent: same value is fine.
  91:             if existing.user_id == entry.user_id and existing.pairing_key == entry.pairing_key:
  92:                 return
  93:             raise BrokerStorageConflictError(
  94:                 f"pairing_id {pairing_id} already completed with different values",
  95:             )
  96: 
  97:     def fetch(self, pairing_id: str) -> BrokerEntry | None:
  98:         with self._lock:
  99:             return self._entries.get(pairing_id)
 100:

 103:     "BrokerEntry",
 104:     "BrokerStorage",
 105:     "BrokerStorageConflictError",
 106:     "InMemoryBrokerStorage",
 107: ]

  16: def _canon_uuid(value: str) -> str:
  17:     """Normalize a UUID string to lowercase no-brace canonical form.
  18:

  36: )
  37: from syncler.errors import (
  38:     PairingConflictError,
  39:     PairingExpiredError,
  40:     PluginRevokedError,
  41:     RecipientUnreachableError,
  42:     SignatureError,

  46: 
  47: DEFAULT_BASE_URL = "https://api.syncler.app"
  48: 
  49: 
  50: @dataclass
  51: class Pairing:
  52:     pairing_id: str
  53:     user_id: str  # the recipient's user UUID after pairing completes
  54: 
  55: 
  56: @dataclass
  57: class SendResult:
  58:     message_id: str
  59:     expires_at: str
  60: 
  61: 
  62: class Client:
  63:     """Thin sync wrapper over the Syncler server REST API.
  64: 
  65:     Usage::
  66: 
  67:         client = Client(
  68:             base_url="https://api.syncler.app",
  69:             sender_name="Trading Bot",
  70:             private_key_path="~/.syncler/keys/trading.pem",
  71:         )
  72:         client.register_if_needed(contact="ops@example.com")
  73: 
  74:         qr_path = client.create_pairing_qr(ttl_seconds=300)
  75:         pairing = client.wait_for_pairing(timeout_seconds=300)
  76: 
  77:         client.send_to(
  78:             user_uuid=pairing.user_id,
  79:             plugin_identifier="com.trading.app",
  80:             payload={"pnl": 1234.56},
  81:             min_plugin_version="1.0.0",
  82:             # pairing_key produced by the device + sender during the
  83:             # bootstrap exchange (M7+; for V1 dev set client.pairing_key
  84:             # directly with a 32-byte shared secret).
  85:         )
  86:     """
  87: 
  88:     def __init__(
  89:         self,
  90:         *,
  91:         sender_name: str,
  92:         private_key_path: str,
  93:         base_url: str = DEFAULT_BASE_URL,
  94:         session: requests.Session | None = None,
  95:         broker_storage: "BrokerStorage | None" = None,
  96:     ):
  97:         self.base_url = base_url.rstrip("/")
  98:         self.sender_name = sender_name
  99:         self.private_key: Ed25519PrivateKey = load_private_key(private_key_path)
 100:         self.public_key = public_key_raw(self.private_key)
 101:         self.session = session or requests.Session()
 102: 
 103:         # State that gets set after register / pairing.
 104:         self.sender_id: str | None = None
 105:         self._pending_pairing_token: str | None = None
 106:         self._pending_pairing_id: str | None = None
 107:         self._latest_pairing: Pairing | None = None
 108:         # V1 per-pairing AES-GCM key. Set automatically by
 109:         # ``wait_for_pairing(...)`` on the V1.5 automated flow; can be
 110:         # set manually via ``set_pairing(...)`` for the V1 manual flow.
 111:         self.pairing_key: bytes | None = None
 112:         # V1.5 Phase 5a-2: broker storage the sender's broker handler
 113:         # writes to AND ``wait_for_pairing(...)`` polls from. None for
 114:         # senders sticking with the V1 manual flow.
 115:         self._broker_storage: "BrokerStorage | None" = broker_storage
 116: 
 117:     # ---------------------------- Sender lifecycle -------------------------
 118: 
 119:     def _canonical_sender_id(self) -> str:
 120:         if self.sender_id is None:
 121:             raise SynclerError("sender_id not set")
 122:         return _canon_uuid(self.sender_id)
 123: 
 124:     def register_if_needed(self, *, contact: str | None = None) -> str:
 125:         """Register the sender public key once. Returns sender_id.
 126: 
 127:         Idempotent: if a server-side row already exists for this public key,
 128:         the server returns 409. The caller is expected to persist
 129:         ``self.sender_id`` between runs; in dev we cache to a JSON file
 130:         beside the private key ג€” but the SDK keeps that detail outside its
 131:         responsibility. For now, the caller catches a 409 themselves.
 132:         """
 133:         body = {
 134:             "public_key": b64(self.public_key),
 135:             "name": self.sender_name,
 136:             "contact": contact,
 137:         }
 138:         resp = self.session.post(f"{self.base_url}/v1/senders/register", json=body, timeout=10)
 139:         if resp.status_code == 409:
 140:             raise SynclerError("sender already registered (use the previously-issued sender_id)")
 141:         resp.raise_for_status()
 142:         self.sender_id = resp.json()["sender_id"]
 143:         return self.sender_id
 144: 
 145:     def set_sender_id(self, sender_id: str) -> None:
 146:         """Set sender_id from a persisted location (after first register)."""

 succeeded in 364ms:
 391: 
 392: The sender generates a static X25519 keypair. It signs the raw 32-byte public key with its Ed25519 signing key to bind the bootstrap identity to the sender identity.
 393: 
 394: Signing input:
 395: ```text
 396: "syncler-v1-bootstrap-key:" (24 bytes ASCII) || bootstrap_pub_x25519 (32 bytes raw)
 397: ```
 398: 
 399: The signature and X25519 public key are registered with the Syncler server. The server stores a hash `bootstrap_key_id = SHA-256(bootstrap_key)[:16]` for stable identification.
 400: 
 401: ### 9.2 Bootstrap Encryption (HPKE-style)
 402: 
 403: The device fetches the sender's bootstrap key and signature from the server and verifies the signature BEFORE proceeding.
 404: 
 405: 1. Device generates an ephemeral X25519 keypair `(eph_priv, eph_pub)`.
 406: 2. `shared_secret = X25519(eph_priv, sender.bootstrap_key)`.
 407: 3. `aead_key = HKDF-SHA256(salt=eph_pub || sender.bootstrap_key, ikm=shared_secret, info="syncler-v1-bootstrap-aead", length=32)`.
 408: 4. `nonce = 12 random bytes`.
 409: 5. `aad = JSON canonical bytes (sorted keys, compact separators, UTF-8)`.
 410: 6. `ciphertext_with_tag = AES-256-GCM(aead_key, nonce, plaintext, aad)`.
 411: 
 412: ### 9.3 Bootstrap AAD
 413: 
 414: Canonical JSON binds the envelope to the specific pairing and broker.
 415: 
 416: ```json
 417: {
 418:   "bootstrap_key_id": "<base64 16 bytes>",
 419:   "exp": "<ISO8601 UTC with Z suffix>",
 420:   "pairing_id": "<uuid>",
 421:   "protocol_version": 1,
 422:   "sender_broker_url": "<string>",
 423:   "sender_id": "<uuid>"
 424: }
 425: ```
 426: 
 427: `sender_broker_url` is named that way (not just `broker_url`) because `PairingInitiateResponse.broker_url` already exists in the V1 wire contract and means "the Syncler-side broker URL the QR encodes" ג€” a different concept. `sender_broker_url` is the URL the sender's backend operates for the encrypted bootstrap POST. Renaming avoids silent semantic overload.
 428: 
 429: **Security Rule:** The broker MUST NOT reconstruct `sender_broker_url` from the envelope. It MUST use the `sender_broker_url` stored in its own pairing state (indexed by `pairing_id`) created when the sender called `pairing/initiate`.
 430: 
 431: ### 9.4 Test Vectors
 432: 
 433: These vectors are asserted by `server/tests/test_crypto.py`.
 434: 
 435: #### Ed25519 Bootstrap Key Signature
 436:

 442: signature: 714def847ce5343f9b06f9263a57e192975709a73a92ae290b8b0eee47770c184eb3c5492d5a8adaed3b459c5614294ea9ddcd64e7b697af2e7b61142f3ac608

 465: ## Equivalents for Android/Kotlin
 466: 
 467: Use platform or vetted library implementations only:
 468: 
 469: ```text
 470: AES-GCM: javax.crypto.Cipher or androidx.security.crypto
 471: Argon2id: BouncyCastle or another maintained Argon2id implementation
 472: Ed25519: BouncyCastle
 473: HKDF-SHA256: BouncyCastle or cryptography library of choice
 474: CSPRNG: java.security.SecureRandom
 475: Canonical JSON: deterministic JSON encoder configured for sorted keys and compact separators

**Codex Reviewer**

Per-area verdict:
- Spec/vectors: **GREEN**. Rename is correctly reflected in the AAD contract and vector text: [docs/crypto-spec.md](D:/Projects/syncler/docs/crypto-spec.md:412), [docs/crypto-spec.md](D:/Projects/syncler/docs/crypto-spec.md:459). Server vector round-trip also tracks the renamed AAD: [server/tests/test_crypto.py](D:/Projects/syncler/server/tests/test_crypto.py:94), [server/tests/test_crypto.py](D:/Projects/syncler/server/tests/test_crypto.py:236).
- Server: **YELLOW**. Shape matches the plan: schema fields are present at [schemas.py](D:/Projects/syncler/server/app/schemas.py:297), migration is nullable at [0008](D:/Projects/syncler/server/alembic/versions/0008_sender_bootstrap_key_and_pending_pairing_broker.py:31), registration endpoint verifies the bootstrap signature at [senders.py](D:/Projects/syncler/server/app/routers/senders.py:88), and initiate requires a registered bootstrap key at [pairing.py](D:/Projects/syncler/server/app/routers/pairing.py:163). But the debug HTTP LAN validator is too loose: prefix matching at [pairing.py](D:/Projects/syncler/server/app/routers/pairing.py:118) accepts DNS names like `127.evil.test` / `localhost.evil.test`.
- Android: **YELLOW**. Crypto builder and AAD helper landed at [BootstrapEnvelope.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/core/crypto/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/core/crypto/BootstrapEnvelope.kt:65), with AAD vector assertion at [SpecVectorsTest.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/core/crypto/src/test/kotlin/app/syncler/core/crypto/SpecVectorsTest.kt:174). But the feature DTO/repository flow is not wired; preview DTO still lacks `sender_broker_url`, `bootstrap_key`, `bootstrap_key_signature`, and `bootstrap_protocol_version`: [SynclerApi.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/core/network/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/core/network/SynclerApi.kt:193), and confirm remains V1-only at [PairingRepository.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/pairing/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/feature/pairing/PairingRepository.kt:53).
- SDK: **YELLOW/GREEN**. Core helpers and CAS storage are reasonable: [bootstrap.py](D:/Projects/syncler/sdk-python/syncler/bootstrap.py:58), [bootstrap.py](D:/Projects/syncler/sdk-python/syncler/bootstrap.py:99), [broker_storage.py](D:/Projects/syncler/sdk-python/syncler/broker_storage.py:69). Client API additions match the plan at [client.py](D:/Projects/syncler/sdk-python/syncler/client.py:151), [client.py](D:/Projects/syncler/sdk-python/syncler/client.py:196), [client.py](D:/Projects/syncler/sdk-python/syncler/client.py:226). Optional broker app is not present, and `pyproject.toml` only has `dev` extras at [pyproject.toml](D:/Projects/syncler/sdk-python/pyproject.toml:13), so don’t describe `syncler[broker]` as shipped.

Option vote: **Option A, but commit after a small fix list**. I would not hold for the Android UX. The byte contract, server fields, endpoint, and SDK crypto are the important semantic pieces and can land as a protocol-foundation commit. The Android UX can be 5a-2.1 because it consumes the contract rather than changing it.

Blockers before commit:
1. Fix `_validate_sender_broker_url` debug HTTP host validation. Use `ipaddress.ip_address(host)` for IP literals plus exact `localhost`; do not allow prefix-matched DNS names.
2. Add targeted server tests for the new endpoint and pairing behavior. The endpoint is security-sensitive enough that “imports clean” is not enough. Minimum: register success, bad bootstrap signature, revoked sender, rotate/overwrite, initiate rejects URL without key, preview surfaces all four bootstrap fields together.
3. Clean the odd typo workaround in [test_crypto.py](D:/Projects/syncler/server/tests/test_crypto.py:243). It passes, but it should simply assert `BOOTSTRAP_ED25519_PUB_HEX`.

Commit framing:
```text
Phase 5a-2: add automated pairing protocol foundation

- rename bootstrap AAD field to sender_broker_url and regenerate vectors
- add sender bootstrap-key registration endpoint and pending pairing URL storage
- surface bootstrap preview fields behind registered sender keys
- add Android bootstrap envelope crypto helper and vector coverage
- add Python SDK bootstrap decrypt helpers, broker storage, and polling client APIs

Deferred to Phase 5a-2.1:
- Android PairingRepository automated POST + fallback banner
- optional syncler[broker] FastAPI helper
- integration-guide automated-flow walkthrough
```

- Spec/server/SDK crypto: **GREEN with test caveat**. The main contract is coherent and matches Consultation 74.
- Android app flow: **YELLOW**. Missing UX means this is not end-to-end exercisable on device.
- Docs/example broker: **YELLOW**. Acceptable as follow-up if explicitly called out.

Option vote: **Option A**. The current commit is valuable if framed as “protocol foundation,” not “complete automated pairing UX.”

**Overall**

Do not label this as fully complete Phase 5a-2 end-to-end. Land it as the protocol/server/SDK/crypto foundation, then make 5a-2.1 the Android repository POST path, broker helper, and integration-guide update.
